2.4.4 Formål med lenke (9 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
MINOR

Link text has redundant phrase: 'Gå til innhold'

<a class="ih6PM2XpnPnHlvxJXeyq" href="#mainContent">Gå til innhold</a>
Remove 'link to' or similar - screen readers already announce it as a link
Testregel 2.4.4 (2.4.4 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Link text is not descriptive: 'Les mer'

<a class="XezMfDvRba8HKhHr79wm B5Z4_vbRcPt248iwmQXi gYkAa9g2NSCw73nq6w8P" data-owned="" href="/aktuelt/opptaksprovene-er-ikke-noe-a-vare-redd-for/" title="Les mer"><div class="DdPYOTimBd1c8zDeoFgi"><s

2.1.1 Tastatur (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.1.1 (2.1.1 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Interactive button has tabindex='-1' - not keyboard accessible

<button aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="true" class="brFFOiXiOEgw5BeGVovg ZAgNSffGchMZ_tZy4qy2 DTuGnl1WKyMu475BbUvg" tabindex="-1" type="button"><span class="visuallyHidden">Åpne søk</span><span
Remove tabindex='-1' unless element is in an inactive state
4.1.2 Navn, rolle, verdi (1 avvik)
Testregel 4.1.2 (4.1.2 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

iframe is missing title attribute

<iframe allow="autoplay; fullscreen" data-ready="true" height="480" loading="lazy" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/svnDTqGpKHU" width="640"></iframe>
Add descriptive title attribute to iframe
